pꜣ gy n ỉri̯=f wp-st|The way of doing it; in detail:
ỉw=k wꜣḥ 1/8 r 1 □ r 1 1/8|You should add 1/8 to 1, □ makes 1 1/8.
ỉw=k ḏd 1/8 pꜣ ỉh̭ (n) <1> 1/8 pꜣỉ r pꜣy=f 1/9|You should say: "What is 1/8 of <1> 1/8?", makes its 1/9.
ỉw=k ḏd 1/8 n wꜣḥ 1/9 n šꜥṱ|You should say: "1/8 is the plus, 1/9 is the proportion (of the total)".

pꜣ g⸢y⸣ n ỉri̯=f wp-st|The way of doing it; in detail:
